
# Third-party licenses

Miku Push! is built using several open-source libraries, runtimes, and frameworks. You can find their licenses listed below, organized by license.

There are packages with multiple licenses. The licenses are listed in the order they appear in the package.

## Licences of all packages

- [MIT](#mit)
- [Apache-2.0](#apache-20)
- [Unicode-3.0](#unicode-30)
- [Unlicense](#unlicense)
- [BSD-2-Clause](#bsd-2-clause)
- [BSD-3-Clause](#bsd-3-clause)
- [Zlib](#zlib)
- [ISC](#isc)
- [BSL-1.0](#bsl-10)
- [MPL-2.0](#mpl-20)
- [CC0-1.0](#cc0-10)
- [MIT-0](#mit-0)
- [0BSD](#0bsd)
- [CDLA-Permissive-2.0](#cdla-permissive-20)
- [CC-BY-4.0](#cc-by-40)
- [Python-2.0](#python-20)
- [BlueOak-1.0.0](#blueoak-100)
- [CC-BY-3.0](#cc-by-30)
